# Add Evaluation Latency Tracking

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Your Team:** Evaluation Team
**Access Scope:** You own `internal/server/evaluation/`. You may read other packages to understand codebase patterns and interfaces, but all code changes must stay within your package.

## Context

You are a developer on the Flipt Evaluation Team. Your team is responsible for the feature flag evaluation engine that determines flag variant assignments. Other teams own storage, analytics, middleware, transport, and configuration — you may read their code to understand patterns, but must not modify their packages.

## Feature Request

**From:** VP Engineering
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** Preparing for SOC 2 compliance — we need observability into evaluation performance

We need to track how long feature flag evaluations take so we can set SLOs and identify performance regressions. Currently, we have no visibility into evaluation latency — when users report slow flag evaluations, we have no data to diagnose the issue.

Add a duration tracking component to the evaluation engine that:
- Records the wall-clock duration of each evaluation
- Provides aggregate statistics: total count, average duration, and P99 latency
- Is safe for concurrent use (our evaluation server handles many simultaneous gRPC requests)

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. Create a new file for duration tracking in the evaluation package with a struct that records durations and retrieves statistics (count, average, P99)
2. Thread-safe implementation
3. Integrate the tracker into the evaluation server — wire it into all evaluation methods (boolean, variant, and batch)
4. All changes within `internal/server/evaluation/`
5. Code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

## Success Criteria

- A duration tracking file exists in the evaluation package
- Thread-safe implementation using appropriate synchronization
- Server struct integrates the tracker
- Evaluation methods record durations
- Go code compiles
- No changes outside `internal/server/evaluation/`

     1→package evaluation
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→
     6→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
     7→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
     8→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
     9→	"go.uber.org/zap"
    10→	"google.golang.org/grpc"
    11→)
    12→
    13→// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
    17→	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {
    23→	logger    *zap.Logger
    24→	store     Storer
    25→	evaluator *Evaluator
    26→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    27→}
    28→
    29→// New is constructs a new Server.
    30→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
    31→	return &Server{
    32→		logger:    logger,
    33→		store:     store,
    34→		evaluator: NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    35→	}
    36→}
    37→
    38→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    39→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    40→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    41→}
    42→
    43→func (s *Server) AllowsNamespaceScopedAuthentication(ctx context.Context) bool {
    44→	return true
    45→}
    46→

    23→// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
    24→// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
    25→func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
    26→	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
    27→	if err != nil {
    28→		return nil, err
    29→	}
    30→
    31→	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))
    32→
    33→	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
    34→	if err != nil {
    35→		return nil, err
    36→	}
    37→
    38→	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
    39→		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
    40→		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
    41→		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
    42→		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
    43→		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
    44→		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
    45→		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
    46→		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
    47→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
    48→		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
    49→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
    50→	}
    51→
    52→	// add otel attributes to span
    53→	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
    54→	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)
    55→
    56→	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("response", resp))
    57→	return resp, nil
    58→}

   264→// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.
   265→func (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {
   266→	resp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{
   267→		Responses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),
   268→	}
   269→
   270→	for _, req := range b.GetRequests() {
   271→		f, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(b.Reference)))
   272→		if err != nil {
   273→			var errnf errs.ErrNotFound
   274→			if errors.As(err, &errnf) {
   275→				eresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{
   276→					Type: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,
   277→					Response: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_ErrorResponse{
   278→						ErrorResponse: &rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationResponse{
   279→							FlagKey:      req.FlagKey,
   280→							NamespaceKey: req.NamespaceKey,
   281→							Reason:       rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationReason_NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON,
   282→						},
   283→					},
   284→				}
   285→
   286→				resp.Responses = append(resp.Responses, eresp)
   287→				continue
   288→			}
   289→
   290→			return nil, err
   291→		}
   292→
   293→		switch f.Type {
   294→		case flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE:
   295→			res, err := s.boolean(ctx, f, req)
   296→			if err != nil {
   297→				return nil, err

     0→package evaluation
     1→
     2→import (
     3→	"sort"
     4→	"sync"
     5→	"time"
     6→)
     7→
     8→// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics.
     9→// It is safe for concurrent use.
    10→type DurationTracker struct {
    11→	mu        sync.RWMutex
    12→	durations []time.Duration
    13→}
    14→
    15→// Record records a single evaluation duration.
    16→func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(duration time.Duration) {
    17→	dt.mu.Lock()
    18→	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
    19→	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, duration)
    20→}
    21→
    22→// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
    23→func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
    24→	dt.mu.RLock()
    25→	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
    26→	return len(dt.durations)
    27→}
    28→
    29→// Average returns the average duration of all recorded evaluations.

    13→// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
    17→	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {
    23→	logger           *zap.Logger
    24→	store            Storer
    25→	evaluator        *Evaluator
    26→	durationTracker  *DurationTracker
    27→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    28→}
    29→
    30→// New is constructs a new Server.
    31→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
    32→	return &Server{
    33→		logger:          logger,
    34→		store:           store,
    35→		evaluator:       NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    36→		durationTracker: &DurationTracker{},
    37→	}
    38→}
    39→
    40→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    41→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    42→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    43→}

    23→// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
    24→// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
    25→func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
    26→	startTime := time.Now()
    27→	defer func() {
    28→		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
    29→	}()
    30→
    31→	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
    32→	if err != nil {
    33→		return nil, err
    34→	}
    35→
    36→	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))
    37→
    38→	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
    39→	if err != nil {
    40→		return nil, err
    41→	}
    42→
    43→	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
    44→		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
    45→		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),

    47→		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),

    50→		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),

    52→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
    53→		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
    54→		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
    55→	}

149-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully implemented the evaluation latency tracking feature for the Flipt evaluation engine. Here's what was delivered:

## Implementation Summary

### 1. **New File: `duration_tracker.go`**
A thread-safe duration tracking component that:
- Records wall-clock duration of each evaluation using `Record(duration time.Duration)`
- Provides aggregate statistics:
  - `Count()` - total number of evaluations
  - `Average()` - average duration across all evaluations
  - `P99()` - 99th percentile latency for identifying performance regressions
- Uses `sync.RWMutex` for safe concurrent access (handles multiple simultaneous gRPC requests)

### 2. **Modified: `server.go`**
- Added `durationTracker *DurationTracker` field to the `Server` struct
- Initialized tracker in the `New()` constructor

### 3. **Modified: `evaluation.go`**
Integrated duration tracking into all three evaluation methods:
- **Variant()** - Records duration of variant flag evaluations
- **Boolean()** - Records duration of boolean flag evaluations  
- **Batch()** - Records duration of batch evaluations

Each method captures the wall-clock time from start to finish using a deferred function.

### 4. **Tests: `duration_tracker_test.go`**
Comprehensive test suite covering:
- Recording and counting evaluations
- Average and P99 calculation
- Concurrent access verification
- Edge cases (empty tracker)

## Verification Results

✅ **All existing tests pass** (50+ tests including Variant, Boolean, and Batch evaluations)
✅ **Code compiles without errors**
✅ **Thread-safe implementation** verified with concurrent access tests
✅ **Changes contained** within `internal/server/evaluation/` package only

The implementation is production-ready and follows Go best practices with proper mutex usage, clear naming c

i <= 100; i++ {\n\t\ttracker.Record(time.Duration(i) * time.Millisecond)\n\t}\n\n\t// P99 should be approximately at the 99th position\n\t// For 100 items, 99% would be at index 99 (0-indexed), which is 100ms\n\tp99 := tracker.P99()\n\tassert.True(t, p99 >= 99*time.Millisecond && p99 <= 100*time.Millisecond,\n\t\t\"P99 should be approximately at 99th percentile, got %v\", p99)\n}\n\nfunc TestDurationTracker_P99_Empty(t *testing.T) {\n\ttracker := &DurationTracker{}\n\tassert.Equal(t, time.Duration(0), tracker.P99())\n}\n\nfunc TestDurationTracker_ConcurrentAccess(t *testing.T) {\n\ttracker := &DurationTracker{}\n\n\t// Spawn multiple goroutines that record durations\n\tdone := make(chan bool, 10)\n\n\tfor i := 0; i < 10; i++ {\n\t\tgo func(id int) {\n\t\t\tfor j := 0; j < 100; j++ {\n\t\t\t\ttracker.Record(time.Duration(j) * time.Millisecond)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdone <- true\n\t\t}(i)\n\t}\n\n\t// Wait for all goroutines to finish\n\tfor i := 0; 1. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/duration_tracker.go
package evaluation

import (
	"sort"
	"sync"
	"time"
)

// DurationTracker records evaluation durations and provides aggregate statistics.
// It is safe for concurrent use.
type DurationTracker struct {
	mu        sync.RWMutex
	durations []time.Duration
}

// Record records a single evaluation duration.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Record(duration time.Duration) {
	dt.mu.Lock()
	defer dt.mu.Unlock()
	dt.durations = append(dt.durations, duration)
}

// Count returns the total number of recorded evaluations.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Count() int {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()
	return len(dt.durations)
}

// Average returns the average duration of all recorded evaluations.
// Returns 0 if no evaluations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) Average() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	var total int64
	for _, d := range dt.durations {
		total += int64(d)
	}

	return time.Duration(total / int64(len(dt.durations)))
}

// P99 returns the 99th percentile duration.
// Returns 0 if no evaluations have been recorded.
func (dt *DurationTracker) P99() time.Duration {
	dt.mu.RLock()
	defer dt.mu.RUnlock()

	if len(dt.durations) == 0 {
		return 0
	}

	// Create a copy to avoid modifying the original slice
	durations := make([]time.Duration, len(dt.durations))
	copy(durations, dt.durations)

	// Sort the durations
	sort.Slice(durations, func(i, j int) bool {
		return durations[i] < durations[j]
	})

	// Calculate the 99th percentile index
	// For n elements, the 99th percentile is at index ceil(0.99 * n) - 1
	index := (len(durations) * 99 / 100)
	if index >= len(durations) {
		index = len(durations) - 1
	}

	return durations[index]
}

// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))

	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
	}

	// add otel attributes to span
	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)

	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("response", resp))
	return resp, nil
}
After
// Variant evaluates a request for a multi-variate flag and entity.
// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("request", r))

	resp, err := s.variant(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
	}

	// add otel attributes to span
	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)

	s.logger.Debug("variant", zap.Stringer("response", resp))
	return resp, nil
}

// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {
	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	s.logger.Debug("boolean", zap.Stringer("request", r))

	if flag.Type != flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE {
		return nil, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
	}

	resp, err := s.boolean(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.Bool(resp.Enabled),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(strconv.FormatBool(resp.Enabled)),
	}

	// add otel attributes to span
	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)

	s.logger.Debug("boolean", zap.Stringer("response", resp))
	return resp, nil
}
After
// Boolean evaluates a request for a boolean flag and entity.
func (s *Server) Boolean(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(r.Reference)))
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	s.logger.Debug("boolean", zap.Stringer("request", r))

	if flag.Type != flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE {
		return nil, errs.ErrInvalidf("flag type %s invalid", flag.Type)
	}

	resp, err := s.boolean(ctx, flag, r)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	spanAttrs := []attribute.KeyValue{
		fliptotel.AttributeNamespace.String(r.NamespaceKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlag.String(r.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.Bool(resp.Enabled),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(r.FlagKey),

}

// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.
func (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {
	resp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{
		Responses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),
	}
After
// Batch takes in a list of *evaluation.EvaluationRequest and returns their respective responses.
func (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {
	startTime := time.Now()
	defer func() {
		s.durationTracker.Record(time.Since(startTime))
	}()

	resp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{
		Responses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),
	}
7. WRITE /workspace/internal/server/evaluation/duration_tracker_test.go
package evaluation

import (
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
)

func TestDurationTracker_Record(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}

	// Record some durations
	tracker.Record(100 * time.Millisecond)
	tracker.Record(200 * time.Millisecond)
	tracker.Record(150 * time.Millisecond)

	// Verify count
	assert.Equal(t, 3, tracker.Count())
}

func TestDurationTracker_Count_Empty(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}
	assert.Equal(t, 0, tracker.Count())
}

func TestDurationTracker_Average(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}

	tracker.Record(100 * time.Millisecond)
	tracker.Record(200 * time.Millisecond)
	tracker.Record(300 * time.Millisecond)

	// Average should be 200ms
	expected := 200 * time.Millisecond
	assert.Equal(t, expected, tracker.Average())
}

func TestDurationTracker_Average_Empty(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}
	assert.Equal(t, time.Duration(0), tracker.Average())
}

func TestDurationTracker_P99(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}

	// Create a dataset where we know the 99th percentile
	// Adding 100 values from 1ms to 100ms
	for i := 1; i <= 100; i++ {
		tracker.Record(time.Duration(i) * time.Millisecond)
	}

	// P99 should be approximately at the 99th position
	// For 100 items, 99% would be at index 99 (0-indexed), which is 100ms
	p99 := tracker.P99()
	assert.True(t, p99 >= 99*time.Millisecond && p99 <= 100*time.Millisecond,
		"P99 should be approximately at 99th percentile, got %v", p99)
}

func TestDurationTracker_P99_Empty(t *testing.T) {
	tracker := &DurationTracker{}
	assert.Equal(t, time.Duration(0), tracker.P99())
}
